Available parameters:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired Parameter:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003einput\u003c/strong\u003e (string): The text to be converted to audio (up to 4096 characters).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOptional Parameters:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003emodel\u003c/strong\u003e (string): Set to \"tts-1\" or \"tts-1-hd\" (default: \u003ccode\u003e\"tts-1\"\u003c/code\u003e).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003evoice\u003c/strong\u003e (string): One of the OpenAI-compatible voices (alloy, echo, fable, onyx, nova, shimmer) or any valid \u003ccode\u003eedge-tts\u003c/code\u003e voice (default: \u003ccode\u003e\"en-US-AndrewNeural\"\u003c/code\u003e).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eresponse_format\u003c/strong\u003e (string): Audio format. Options: \u003ccode\u003emp3\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eopus\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eaac\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eflac\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ewav\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003epcm\u003c/code\u003e (default: \u003ccode\u003emp3\u003c/code\u003e).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003espeed\u003c/strong\u003e (number): Playback speed (0.25 to 4.0). Default is \u003ccode\u003e1.0\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eExample request with \u003ccode\u003ecurl\u003c/code\u003e and saving the output to an mp3 file:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"curl -X POST http://localhost:5050/v1/audio/speech \\\n  -H \u0026quot;Content-Type: application/json\u0026quot; \\\n  -H \u0026quot;Authorization: Bearer your_api_key_here\u0026quot; \\\n  -d '{\n    \u0026quot;input\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;Hello, I am your AI assistant! <a href="https://img.shields.io/github/sponsors/travisvn" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/6d24ad1fc18fa9d263cacee4c5d9aa8e15128bd5f3f3184f6f54d20e6a4ab63b/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f7374617469632f76313f6c6162656c3d53706f6e736f72266d6573736167653d254532253944254134266c6f676f3d47697448756226636f6c6f723d253233666538653836" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/static/v1?label=Sponsor&amp;message=%E2%9D%A4&amp;logo=GitHub&amp;color=%23fe8e86" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">This project provides a local, OpenAI-compatible text-to-speech (TTS) API using <code>edge-tts</code>. It emulates the OpenAI TTS endpoint (<code>/v1/audio/speech</code>), enabling users to generate speech from text with various voice options and playback speeds, just like the OpenAI API.</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>edge-tts</code> uses Microsoft Edge's online text-to-speech service, so it is completely free.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://hub.docker.com/r/travisvn/openai-edge-tts" rel="nofollow">View this project on Docker Hub</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Please 猸锔 star this repo if you find it helpful</h1><a id="user-content-please-锔-star-this-repo-if-you-find-it-helpful" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Please 猸锔 star this repo if you find it helpful" href="#please-锔-star-this-repo-if-you-find-it-helpful"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Features</h2><a id="user-content-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Features" href="#features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>OpenAI-Compatible Endpoint</strong>: <code>/v1/audio/speech</code> with similar request structure and behavior.</li>
<li><strong>Supported Voices</strong>: Maps OpenAI voices (alloy, echo, fable, onyx, nova, shimmer) to <code>edge-tts</code> equivalents.</li>
<li><strong>Flexible Formats</strong>: Supports multiple audio formats (mp3, opus, aac, flac, wav, pcm).</li>
<li><strong>Adjustable Speed</strong>: Option to modify playback speed (0.25x to 4.0x).</li>
<li><strong>Optional Direct Edge-TTS Voice Selection</strong>: Use either OpenAI voice mappings or specify any edge-tts voice directly.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Getting Started</h2><a id="user-content-getting-started" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Getting Started" href="#getting-started"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Prerequisites</h3><a id="user-content-prerequisites" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Prerequisites" href="#prerequisites"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Docker</strong> (recommended): Docker and Docker Compose for containerized setup.</li>
<li><strong>Python</strong> (optional): For local development, install dependencies in <code>requirements.txt</code>.</li>
<li><strong>ffmpeg</strong>: Required for audio format conversion and playback speed adjustments.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h3><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Clone the Repository</strong>:</li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="git clone https://github.com/travisvn/openai-edge-tts.git
cd openai-edge-tts"><pre>git clone https://github.com/travisvn/openai-edge-tts.git
<span class="pl-c1">cd</span> openai-edge-tts</pre></div>
<ol start="2" dir="auto">
<li><strong>Environment Variables</strong>: Create a <code>.env</code> file in the root directory with the following variables:</li>
</ol>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="API_KEY=your_api_key_here
PORT=5050

DEFAULT_VOICE=en-US-AndrewNeural
DEFAULT_RESPONSE_FORMAT=mp3
DEFAULT_SPEED=1.0

DEFAULT_LANGUAGE=en-US

REQUIRE_API_KEY=True"><pre class="notranslate"><code>API_KEY=your_api_key_here
PORT=5050

DEFAULT_VOICE=en-US-AndrewNeural
DEFAULT_RESPONSE_FORMAT=mp3
DEFAULT_SPEED=1.0

DEFAULT_LANGUAGE=en-US

REQUIRE_API_KEY=True
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Or, copy the default <code>.env.example</code> with the following:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cp .env.example .env"><pre>cp .env.example .env</pre></div>
<ol start="3" dir="auto">
<li><strong>Run with Docker Compose</strong> (recommended):</li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="docker compose up --build"><pre>docker compose up --build</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>(Note: docker-compose is not the same as docker compose)</em></p>
<p dir="auto">Run with <code>-d</code> to run docker compose in "detached mode", meaning it will run in the background and free up your terminal.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="docker compose up -d"><pre>docker compose up -d</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, <strong>run directly with Docker</strong>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="docker build -t openai-edge-tts .
docker run -p 5050:5050 --env-file .env openai-edge-tts"><pre>docker build -t openai-edge-tts <span class="pl-c1">.</span>
docker run -p 5050:5050 --env-file .env openai-edge-tts</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">To run the container in the background, add <code>-d</code> after the <code>docker run</code> command:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="docker run -d -p 5050:5050 --env-file .env openai-edge-tts"><pre>docker run -d -p 5050:5050 --env-file .env openai-edge-tts</pre></div>
<ol start="4" dir="auto">
<li><strong>Access the API</strong>: Your server will be accessible at <code>http://localhost:5050</code>.</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Running with Python</h2><a id="user-content-running-with-python" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Running with Python" href="#running-with-python"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you prefer to run this project directly with Python, follow these steps to set up a virtual environment, install dependencies, and start the server.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Clone the Repository</h3><a id="user-content-1-clone-the-repository" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Clone the Repository" href="#1-clone-the-repository"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="git clone https://github.com/travisvn/openai-edge-tts.git
cd openai-edge-tts"><pre>git clone https://github.com/travisvn/openai-edge-tts.git
<span class="pl-c1">cd</span> openai-edge-tts</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Set Up a Virtual Environment</h3><a id="user-content-2-set-up-a-virtual-environment" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Set Up a Virtual Environment" href="#2-set-up-a-virtual-environment"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Create and activate a virtual environment to isolate dependencies:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# For macOS/Linux
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate

# For Windows
python -m venv venv
venv\Scripts\activate"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> For macOS/Linux</span>
python3 -m venv venv
<span class="pl-c1">source</span> venv/bin/activate

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> For Windows</span>
python -m venv venv
venv<span class="pl-cce">\S</span>cripts<span class="pl-cce">\a</span>ctivate</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">3. Install Dependencies</h3><a id="user-content-3-install-dependencies" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 3. Install Dependencies" href="#3-install-dependencies"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Use <code>pip</code> to install the required packages listed in <code>requirements.txt</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pip install -r requirements.txt"><pre>pip install -r requirements.txt</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. Configure Environment Variables</h3><a id="user-content-4-configure-environment-variables" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4. Configure Environment Variables" href="#4-configure-environment-variables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Create a <code>.env</code> file in the root directory and set the following variables:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="API_KEY=your_api_key_here
PORT=5050

DEFAULT_VOICE=en-US-AndrewNeural
DEFAULT_RESPONSE_FORMAT=mp3
DEFAULT_SPEED=1.0

DEFAULT_LANGUAGE=en-US

REQUIRE_API_KEY=True"><pre lang="plaintext" class="notranslate"><code>API_KEY=your_api_key_here
PORT=5050

DEFAULT_VOICE=en-US-AndrewNeural
DEFAULT_RESPONSE_FORMAT=mp3
DEFAULT_SPEED=1.0

DEFAULT_LANGUAGE=en-US

REQUIRE_API_KEY=True
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5. Run the Server</h3><a id="user-content-5-run-the-server" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5. Run the Server" href="#5-run-the-server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Once configured, start the server with:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python app/server.py"><pre>python app/server.py</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The server will start running at <code>http://localhost:5050</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">6. Test the API</h3><a id="user-content-6-test-the-api" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 6. Test the API" href="#6-test-the-api"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can now interact with the API at <code>http://localhost:5050/v1/audio/speech</code> and other available endpoints. See the <a href="#usage">Usage</a> section for request examples.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Usage</h3><a id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Usage" href="#usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Endpoint: <code>/v1/audio/speech</code></h4><a id="user-content-endpoint-v1audiospeech" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Endpoint: /v1/audio/speech" href="#endpoint-v1audiospeech"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Generates audio from the input text. Available parameters:</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Required Parameter:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>input</strong> (string): The text to be converted to audio (up to 4096 characters).</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Optional Parameters:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>model</strong> (string): Set to "tts-1" or "tts-1-hd" (default: <code>"tts-1"</code>).</li>
<li><strong>voice</strong> (string): One of the OpenAI-compatible voices (alloy, echo, fable, onyx, nova, shimmer) or any valid <code>edge-tts</code> voice (default: <code>"en-US-AndrewNeural"</code>).</li>
<li><strong>response_format</strong> (string): Audio format. Options: <code>mp3</code>, <code>opus</code>, <code>aac</code>, <code>flac</code>, <code>wav</code>, <code>pcm</code> (default: <code>mp3</code>).</li>
<li><strong>speed</strong> (number): Playback speed (0.25 to 4.0). Default is <code>1.0</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Example request with <code>curl</code> and saving the output to an mp3 file:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="curl -X POST http://localhost:5050/v1/audio/speech \
  -H &quot;Content-Type: application/json&quot; \
  -H &quot;Authorization: Bearer your_api_key_here&quot; \
  -d '{
    &quot;input&quot;: &quot;Hello, I am your AI assistant! Just let me know how I can help bring your ideas to life.&quot;,
    &quot;voice&quot;: &quot;echo&quot;,
    &quot;response_format&quot;: &quot;mp3&quot;,
    &quot;speed&quot;: 1.0
  }' \
  --output speech.mp3"><pre>curl -X POST http://localhost:5050/v1/audio/speech \
  -H <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Content-Type: application/json<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> \
  -H <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Authorization: Bearer your_api_key_here<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> \
  -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "input": "Hello, I am your AI assistant! Just let me know how I can help bring your ideas to life.",</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "voice": "echo",</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "response_format": "mp3",</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "speed": 1.0</span>
<span class="pl-s">  }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> \
  --output speech.mp3</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Or, to be in line with the OpenAI API endpoint parameters:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="curl -X POST http://localhost:5050/v1/audio/speech \
  -H &quot;Content-Type: application/json&quot; \
  -H &quot;Authorization: Bearer your_api_key_here&quot; \
  -d '{
    &quot;model&quot;: &quot;tts-1&quot;,
    &quot;input&quot;: &quot;Hello, I am your AI assistant! Just let me know how I can help bring your ideas to life.&quot;,
    &quot;voice&quot;: &quot;alloy&quot;
  }' \
  --output speech.mp3"><pre>curl -X POST http://localhost:5050/v1/audio/speech \
  -H <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Content-Type: application/json<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> \
  -H <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Authorization: Bearer your_api_key_here<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> \
  -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "model": "tts-1",</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "input": "Hello, I am your AI assistant! Just let me know how I can help bring your ideas to life.",</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "voice": "alloy"</span>
<span class="pl-s">  }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> \
  --output speech.mp3</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">And an example of a language other than English:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="curl -X POST http://localhost:5050/v1/audio/speech \
  -H &quot;Content-Type: application/json&quot; \
  -H &quot;Authorization: Bearer your_api_key_here&quot; \
  -d '{
    &quot;model&quot;: &quot;tts-1&quot;,
    &quot;input&quot;: &quot;琛昏瑾裤广&quot;,
    &quot;voice&quot;: &quot;ja-JP-KeitaNeural&quot;
  }' \
  --output speech.mp3"><pre>curl -X POST http://localhost:5050/v1/audio/speech \
  -H <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Content-Type: application/json<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> \
  -H <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Authorization: Bearer your_api_key_here<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> \
  -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "model": "tts-1",</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "input": "琛昏瑾裤广",</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "voice": "ja-JP-KeitaNeural"</span>
<span class="pl-s">  }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> \
  --output speech.mp3</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Additional Endpoints</h3><a id="user-content-additional-endpoints" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Additional Endpoints" href="#additional-endpoints"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>POST/GET /v1/models</strong>: Lists available TTS models.</li>
<li><strong>POST/GET /v1/voices</strong>: Lists <code>edge-tts</code> voices for a given language / locale.</li>
<li><strong>POST/GET /v1/voices/all</strong>: Lists all <code>edge-tts</code> voices, with language support information.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Contributing</h3><a id="user-content-contributing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Contributing" href="#contributing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Contributions are welcome! Please fork the repository and create a pull request for any improvements.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Example Use Case</h2><a id="user-content-example-use-case" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example Use Case" href="#example-use-case"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Open WebUI</h1><a id="user-content-open-webui" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Open WebUI" href="#open-webui"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Open up the Admin Panel and go to Settings -&gt; Audio</p>
<p dir="auto">Below, you can see a screenshot of the correct configuration for using this project to substitute the OpenAI endpoint</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/e70318520a15a154affa6a8218f979ac69c8aa14ce7f89c4360d8b0bc1a9d516/68747470733a2f2f757466732e696f2f662f4d4d4d48695131545161426f5132416e5068556c5444477452344232763745394a5a4e315055356e4173656f61584963"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/e70318520a15a154affa6a8218f979ac69c8aa14ce7f89c4360d8b0bc1a9d516/68747470733a2f2f757466732e696f2f662f4d4d4d48695131545161426f5132416e5068556c5444477452344232763745394a5a4e315055356e4173656f61584963" alt="Screenshot of Open WebUI Admin Settings for Audio adding the correct endpoints for this project" data-canonical-src="https://utfs.io/f/MMMHiQ1TQaBoQ2AnPhUlTDGtR4B2v7E9JZN1PU5nAseoaXIc" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">AnythingLLM</h1><a id="user-content-anythingllm" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: AnythingLLM" href="#anythingllm"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In version 1.6.8, AnythingLLM added support for "generic OpenAI TTS providers"  meaning we can use this project as the TTS provider in AnythingLLM</p>
<p dir="auto">Open up settings and go to Voice &amp; Speech (Under AI Providers)</p>
<p dir="auto">Below, you can see a screenshot of the correct configuration for using this project to substitute the OpenAI endpoint</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/2ce415ced8c3e80d281b644596fcbdcd7a19f6673a2708292333728609097e1b/68747470733a2f2f757466732e696f2f662f4d4d4d48695131545161426f47783657555452444a5557504c716f4d7358694e6b616a4164564f776763784836757637"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/2ce415ced8c3e80d281b644596fcbdcd7a19f6673a2708292333728609097e1b/68747470733a2f2f757466732e696f2f662f4d4d4d48695131545161426f47783657555452444a5557504c716f4d7358694e6b616a4164564f776763784836757637" alt="Screenshot of AnythingLLM settings for Voice adding the correct endpoints for this project" data-canonical-src="https://utfs.io/f/MMMHiQ1TQaBoGx6WUTRDJUWPLqoMsXiNkajAdVOwgcxH6uv7" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quick Info</h2><a id="user-content-quick-info" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quick Info" href="#quick-info"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>your_api_key_here</code> never needs to be replaced  No "real" API key is required. Use whichever string you'd like.</li>
<li>The quickest way to get this up and running is to install docker and run the command below:</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="docker run -d -p 5050:5050 -e API_KEY=your_api_key_here -e PORT=5050 travisvn/openai-edge-tts:latest"><pre>docker run -d -p 5050:5050 -e API_KEY=your_api_key_here -e PORT=5050 travisvn/openai-edge-tts:latest</pre></div>
